## log " AX620E small-encoder build"

```
pulsar2 build --input small-encoder.onnx \
    --config config_whisper_encoder_u16.json \
    --output_dir small_encoder \
    --output_name small-encoder.axmodel \
    --target_hardware AX620E \
    --compiler.check 0 2>&1 
```

```
pulsar2 build --input small-encoder.onnx \
    --config config_whisper_encoder_u16.json \
    --output_dir small_encoder \
    --output_name small-encoder.axmodel \
    --target_hardware AX650 \
    --compiler.check 0 2>&1
```
